\bentry
\wordRemoveSpace{V-v}{V v}
\pron{viV} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{Vs} yA \eng{V's}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} iMgilxSf vaNRmAleya ipapxtetxraDaneya akaSxra. 
\num{2} mara \mo vugaLa paTiTxgaLa \eng{V} AkArada joVDaNe. 
\num{3} \eng{V} AkArada vasutx. 
\num{4} roVmanf saMKAyx saMkeVtadalilx aidu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\pron{vAYxkf}

\bmng

\bentry
\word{vacancy} 
\pron{veVkanisx} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{vacancies}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} baridAgiruvike; KAliyAgiruvike. 
\num{2} shUnayxmanasakxte; jDamanasakxte; manasisxna niSikxrXya sithxti. 
\num{3} KAli hudedx yA sAthxna: \eng{he has no vacancy on his staff} Atana sibabxMdi vagaRdalilx yAva KAli sAthxnavU illx. \eng{no vacancies at present in this office} sadayxdalilx I kaceVriyalilx yAva hudedxgaLU KAli illx. 
\num{4} (hoVTelu \mo vugaLalilx) lBayxviruva KAli koVNe, rUmu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{vacant} 
\pron{veVkaMTf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} baridAgiruva; KAli(yAgiruva); BatiRyAgillxda: \eng{the house is still vacant} A mane inUnx KAli ide. 
\num{2} biDuvAgiruva; yAva kelsavU illxde virAmavAgiruva: \eng{this will amuse your vacant hours} ninanx biDuvAda, virAmada, hotitxnalilx idu ninage vinoVdavanunx koDutatxde. 
\num{3} terapAgiruva; KAli iruva: \eng{he applied for a vacant post} avanu terapAgidadx, KAli idadx, oMdu hudedxgAgi ajiR hAkikoMDa. 
\num{4} shUnayxmanasakxnAda; vicAra, BAva -- shUnayx Ada; niSikxrXya, jDa -- manasakxnAda: \eng{his mind seems completely vacant} avanu saMpUNRvAgi shUnayxmanasakxnaMtidAdxne. \eng{a vacant stare} shUnayxdaqSiTx; gamanakekx tegedukoLaLxde neTTx daqSiTxyiMda elolxV noVDutitxruvudu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\num{3} vAyuviraLate; vAyuvina otatxDa yA saMmadaR sAmAnayxvAgi irabeVkAda parxmANkikxMta kaDimeyAgiruvudu. 
\num{4} aBAva; rAhitayx; yAvudeV sathxLa, saninxveVsha, \mo vugaLalilx irabeVkAda vayxkitx, vasutx, caTuvaTike, \mo vu illxdiruvudu.

\num{3} (\veYshA) habe; auSadhiyAgi usirADuvudakekx baLasuva yAvudeV padAthaR. 
\num{4} poLuLxkalpxne; huruLillxda, nijvallxda -- vasutx yA viSaya; \eng{it's all mere vapoury} adellx bariya poLuLxkalpxne.

\bentry
\word{variety} 
\pron{vareYaTi} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{varieties}). }
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} bagebage(yAgiruvudu); vividhate; veYvidhayx: \eng{variety} \eng{of the scenery} A daqshAyxvaLiya veYvidhayx. \eng{Bangalore has the charm of variety} beMgaLUru nagarakekx veYvidhayxda moVhakate ide. 
\num{2} bahumuKte: \eng{the variety of his conversation} avana saMBASaNeyalilx kaMDubaruva bahumuKte. 
\num{3} bagebageya, vividha, nAnA bageya -- vasutxgaLu yA viSayagaLu yA avugaLa samudAya: \eng{a variety of books} bagebageya pusatxkagaLu. \eng{a variety of reasons} nAnA bageya kAraNgaLu. 
\hypertarget{variety(4)}{} 
\num{4} vividha vinoVdAvaLi; naqtayx, gAyana, hAsAyxBinaya, \mo vugaLa parxdashaRna kAyaRkarxma. 
\num{5} (\jiVvi) upajAti; sAmAnayx lkaSxNgaLalilx parxdhAna jAtivoMdariMda BinanxvAda oMdu upajAti yA adaralolxMdu pArxNi. 
\numi{6} (\jiVvi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} upajAti; oMdeV jAtige seVridudAgi, jAtiyoLage punarutapxtitx sAdhayxviruva, Adare AnuvaMshika lkaSxNgaLu savxlpxmaTiTxge BinanxvAgiruva vayxkitx yA guMpu.

\bentry
\word{vary} 
\pron{veVri} 
\gl{\kirx}(vataRmAna \parxpu\ \Eva\ \eng{varies}; \BU\ matutx 
\BUkaq\ \eng{varied}). \bmng
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} badalAyisu; mApaRDisu; vayxtAyxsagoLisu: \eng{we can vary the pressure at will} otatxDavanunx, saMmadaRvanunx, nAvu beVkAdaMte mApaRDisabahudu. \eng{he seldom varies the routine} dinacariyanunx avanu badalAyisuvudu tiVra viraLa, bahushaH badalAyisuvudillx. \eng{the doctor varies the treatment according to circumstances} veYdayxnu cikitAsxvidhAnavanunx saMdaBoRVcitavAgi vayxtAyxsa mADutAtxne. 
\num{2} veYvidhayxgoLisu: \eng{his style is not sufficiently varied} avana sheYliyalilx sAkaSuTx veYvidhayxvillx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (guN, rUpa, pariNAma, \mo vugaLalilx) badalAyisu; badalAvaNeyAgu; vayxtAyxsavAgu: \eng{his mood varies from day to day} avana manasusx, manaHsithxti dinadiMda dinakekx badalAyisutitxrutatxde. \eng{the temperature varies from} \eng{$30^\circ$} \eng{to} \eng{$70^\circ$} tApamAnavu \eng{$30^\circ$} yiMda \eng{$70^\circ$} ge vayxtAyxsavAgutatxde. 
\num{2} beVreyAgiru; BinanxvAgiru: \eng{this varies from the type} idu tananx jAtiyiMda BinanxvAgide, beVre bageyadAgide. 
\num{3} beVrebeVreyAgiru; bagebageyAgiru; vividhavAgiru; Binanx BinanxvAgiru: \eng{opinions vary on this point} I viSayadalilx aBipArxyagaLu bagebageyAgive, BinanxBinanxvAgive. 
\num{4} anuguNvAgiru; anusAravAgi, anuguNvAgi badalAvaNe hoMdu: \eng{the demand varies with the season} beVDike kAlkekx anuguNvAgirutatxde, anuguNvAgi vayxtAyxsavAgutatxde. 
\num{5} (\ga) (anuloVmavAgi yA viloVmavAgi) badalAyisu; Binanx mwlyxgaLanunx paDe: \eng{attraction of bodies varies directly as their masses and inversely as the square of their distance} kAyagaLa parasapxra AkaSaRNe avugaLa parimANkekx anuloVmavAgi matutx dUrakekx viloVmavAgi vayxtAyxsavAgutatxde, badalAyisutatxde. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word[vegetable(2)]{vegetable} 
\pron{vejiTba(bf)lf, vejfTba(bf)lf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (AhAravAgi baLasuva giDamUlike gaLiMda huTuTxva) shAka; kAyipalyx, tarakAri, sopupx, \mo vu; \udA\, koVsugeDeDx, ele, AlUgeDeDx, badaneVkAyi, beMDekAyi, daMTina sopu px, itAyxdi. 
\num{2} (\AmA) sasayxsadaqsha vayxkitx; (\kanmu\ meduLina hAni \mo vugaLiMda yA utatxma guri \mo vu illxdadxriMda) caTuvaTikeyillxde yA EkatAnavAgi UTniderxgaLalelxV Ayususx savesuvavanu. 
\enum
\emng

\num{3} (\rUpa) (koVpatApa, asahane, \mo\ BAva, aBipArxya, BAvane, \mo vanunx horadoVralu yA vayxkatxpaDisalu baLasuva) vidhAna; upAya; dAri; mAgaR; riVti; avakAsha: \eng{he gave vent to his indignation at such injustice} aMtha anAyxyada viSayadalilx avaniguMTAda nAyxyavAda koVpavanunx avanu vayxkatxpaDisida. \eng{his impatience found a vent in his restless conduct} avana caDapaDikeyalilx avana asahane vayxkatxgoMDitu.

\gl{\gu}

\num{3} keVval shabadxgaLige yA padagaLige saMbaMdhisida: \eng{a purely verbal distinction between two concepts} eraDu kalpxnegaLa naDuvaN keVval shAbidxka vayxtAyxsa. 
\num{4} vAcika; vAgUrxpada; bAyimAtina; mwKika: barahada mUlka Agirade mAtina mUlka tiLisida: \eng{verbal contract} bAyimAtina yA muKtaH mADikoMDa -- karAru, opapxMda. \eng{verbal evidence} bAyimAtina, vAcA heVLida, mwKika -- sAkaSxyX. 
\num{5} (anuvAdada, tajuRmeya \vi) akaSxraniSaThx; padaniSaThx; akaSxrashaH, padashaH -- mADida. 
\num{6} (\vAyx) kirxyA padada yA rUpada: \eng{verbal inflexions} kirxyApadada kAl \eng{(tense)}, parxyoVga \eng{(voice)}, BAva \eng{(mood)}, vacana \eng{(number)} matutx puruSa \eng{(person)} eMba rUpAMtaragaLu yA rUpaBeVdagaLu.

\bentry
\word{verify} 
\pron{veripheY} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{(vataRmAna \parxpu\ \Eva\ \eng{verifies}; \BU\ matutx}
\BUkaq\ \eng{verified}). \bmng
\bnum
\num{1} sari, tALe, tAkaRNe -- noVDu: \eng{always verify your references} ninanx ulelxVKgaLanunx tapapxde sarinoVDu, sariyAgideye eMbaudanunx Kcita mADiko. 
\num{2} parishiVlne, parxyoVga yA pariVkeSxgaLa mUlka viSayavu satayx yA sari eMbaudanunx rujuvAtupaDisu: \eng{I must verify his statement} avana heVLike nijve eMbaudanunx nAnu pariVkiSxsi noVDabeVku. 
\num{3} (GaTne, kAyaR, \mo vugaLa \vi) niriVkaSxNege, vAgAdxna, \mo vakekx -- anuguNvAgiru; niriVkaSxNe, vAgAdxna, \mo vanunx nijpaDisu. 
\numi{4} (\nAyxshA) 
\banum
\alnum{a} dAveyalilx sUcisiruva vAdagaLige yA parxtivAdagaLige keYPiyatatxnunx yA dAKleyanunx lgatitxsu. 
\alnum{b} heVLikeyanunx rujuvAtugaLiMda yA parxmANpatarxdiMda (satayxveMdu) samathiRsu, daqDhapaDisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[very(1)]{very} 
\pron{veri} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\pArxparx) nijvAda; vAsatxvavAda; yathAthaRvAda; sAkASxtAtxda; sAcA: \eng{very God} nijvAda deVvaru. 
\num{2} parama; acacx; apapxT; keVval; shudAdhxMgavAda: \eng{the veriest simpleton knows that} shudadhx muTAThxLanU adanunx ballx. \eng{the very truth} parama satayx. \eng{must consent from very shame} keVval nAcikegAdarU, apakiVtiRya BayakAkxdarU opapxleV beVku. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\eng{the, this, that, his, etc. very} ivaneV, ideV, avaneV, adeV, avana savxMta, itAyxdi athaRgaLalilx avadhAraNAthaRdalilx, otitxheVLuva \parx : \eng{this is the very spot where I found it} nanageadu doreta sathxLa, ideV. \eng{the very same} tadavxtAtxgiadeV. \eng{these were his very words} ivu avana savxMta mAtugaLu; ImAtugaLu avanaveV. \eng{speaking in this very room} I koThaDiyalelxVmAtanADutAtx. \eng{he did it this very day} avanu adanunx ideV dina,iMdeV mADida. \eng{the very fact of his presence is enough} avanuhAjrAgidadx eMba saMgatiyeV sAku. \eng{you are the very man I am looking for} nAnu huDukutitxruva vayxkitx niVneV. \eng{a needle is the very thing for our purpose} namamx udedxVshakekx beVkAda vasutxeMdare sUjiyeV. \eng{come here this very minute} I kaSxN(dalelxV)ililx bA. \eng{it grieves me to the very heart} adu nananxhaqdayAMtarALavanenxV vayxthegoLisutatxde. \eng{the very stones cry out} A kalulxgaLeV kUgi heVLutatxve. \eng{at the very edge of the cliff} A koVDugalilxna tutatx tudiyalilx. \eng{a very little will do} tiVra, keVval savxlpx sAku. \eng{give me only a very little}nanage bahaLa savxlpx, oMdu cuTku mAtarx koDu. \eentry

\bentry
\word[very(2)]{very} 
\pron{veri} 
\gl{\kirxvi}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} (-tamarUpada \gu\ doDane). 
\banum
\alnum{a} atayxMta; kaTTxkaDeya; atayxdhika; gariSaThx; paramAvadhi : \eng{drink it to the very last drop} adanunx kaTTxkaDeya haniyavaregU kuDidubiDu. \eng{the very last thing I expected} (niSeVdhAthaRdalilx mAtarx) nAnu niriVkiSxsidadxralilx atayxMta kaDeyadu (eMdare adanunx nAnu niriVkiSxsiraleV illx). \eng{did the very best I could} nananx keYyalAlxda paramAvadhiyanunx mADide. \eng{did my very utmost} nananx atayxdhika parxyatanxvanUnx mADide. 
\alnum{b} \eng{own} padadoDane\eng{} pUtiRyAgi; saMpUNARthaRdalilx: \eng{my very own room} nananxdeV koVNe. \eng{you may keep it for your very own} adanunx niVnu pUtiR ninanx savxMtakAkxgi iTuTxkoLaLxbahudu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (\gu gaLu, visheVSa kaqdaMtagaLu matutx \kirxvi gaLoDane) tuMba; bahaLa; bahu; balu; tiVra: \eng{that is very easy} adu bahaLa sulBa. \eng{it is very annoying} adu tiVra kirikiriyanunxMTu mADuvaMthadu. \eng{it is very easily done} adanunx bahu sulBavAgi mADabahudu. \eng{it is a very trying time} idu tiVra kaSaTxkaravAda kAl. \eng{it very often fails} adu bahuveVLe viPalvAgutatxde. \eng{we find very few instances} nidashaRnagaLu dorakuvudu tiVra viraLa. \eng{he gives very little trouble} avaniMdAguva sharxma atayxlpx. \eng{is very much better} bahumaTiTxge utatxmavAgidAdxne. \eng{I am very much annoyed} nanage tiVra kirikiriyuMTAgide. 
\enum
\emng

\pron{vesfTxmaMTf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\kanmu\ adhikAra sUcaka) uDupu; vasatxrXvasana; poVSAku. 
\num{2} (\kanmu\ pAdirx \mo varu pArxthaRnA samayadalilx dharisuva) vidhuyxkatx uDupu (\kanmu\ ArAdhane yA parxBuBoVjna saMsAkxradalilx toDuva toVLillxda dagale). 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

 (naDu aMgiya) saNNx jeVbau. 
\emng

\pron{vesiTxrX} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{vestries}). }
\bmng

\numi{2} (\ca) (\birx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (pAYxriSfge saMbaMdhisida viSayagaLanunx caciRsalu pAYxriSf sadasayxru, \kanmu\ caciRna vasAtxrXgAradalilx kUDuva) pAYxriSf saBe. 
\alnum{b} I riVti seVruva pAYxriSf saMGa. 
\eanum
\numie

\emng

\bentry
\word[veto(1)]{veto} 
\pron{viVToV} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{vetoes}). }
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} viVToV; nirAkaraNAdhikAra; anaMgiVkArAdhikAra : 
\banum
\alnum{a} rAj yA rANi, rASATxrXdhayxkaSx, gavanaRrf yA rAjyxpAl, shAsanasaBegaLa peYki meVlina saBe \mo vakekx iruva, keLashAsana saBeyu mADida niNRyavanunx yA shAsanavanunx taLiLxhAkuva adhikAra. 
\alnum{b} vishavxsaMsethxya BadarxtA maMDaliya shAshavxtasadasayx rASaTxrXkekx maMDaliya bahumaMdi sadasayxru aMgiVkarisida niNRyavanUnx saha nirAkarisuva adhikAra. 
\alnum{c} aMtha nirAkaraNe. 
\alnum{d} A nirAkaraNeyanonxLagoMDa saMdeVsha yA sudidx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} taDe; niroVdha; niSeVdha; yAvudeV viSayakekx aDiDxmADuvudu: \eng{he put a (\engit{or} his) veto on the proposal} avanu A salheyanunx niSeVdhisida. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
 \eng{suspensive veto} sathxgana viVToV; niNRyavanunx yA shAsanavanunx tAtAkxlikavAgi taDehiDiyuva, sathxgitagoLisuva viVToV. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[view(1)]{view} 
\pron{vUyx} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} noVT; viVkaSxN; dashaRna; avaloVkana. 
\num{2} (\nAyxshA) (nAyxyadashiR maMDaliyu mokadadxmege saMbaMdhisida sathxLa, Asitx, \mo vanunx yA maqtadeVhavanunx) noVDuvudu; parishiVlne; pariVkaSxN. 
\num{3} daqSiTx; noVT; noVTda, kaNiNxna -- vAyxpitx: \eng{in full view of the crowd} guMpina kaNeNxdurinalelxV. \eng{the bird came into view} A pakiSx noVTda vAyxpitxge baMtu. \eng{the ship passed from our view} A haDagu namamx daqSiTxyiMda sariyitu, kaNmxreyAyitu. 
\num{4} noVT; daqshayx; nidiRSaTx sAthxnadiMda noVDalpxTTxdudx: \eng{the house has a view of the sea} A maneyiMda samudarxda noVT sigutatxde, samudarx kANutatxde. \eng{a superb view} aduBxtavAda oMdu noVT, Bavayxdaqshayx. 
\num{5} daqshayxcitarx; yAvudeV vasutx \mo vugaLa noVTvanunx oLagoMDiruva citarx. 
\num{6} daqSiTx; aBipArxya; BAvane; yAvudeV viSayavanunx -- noVDuva bage, kurita manoVBAva: \eng{he takes a different view} avanu beVre aBipArxyavanunx taLedidAdxne. \eng{his view is that we are aggressors} nAvu AkarxmaNkArareMbaudu avana BAvane. \eng{that is his view of her conduct} avaLa naDavaLikeya viSayadalilx avana daqSiTx adu. \eng{he holds extreme views (in politics etc. )} (rAjkiVya \mo vugaLalilx) avanu tiVvarxgAmi aBipArxyagaLanunx hoMdidAdxne. \eng{took a favourable view of the matter} viSayada bagegx anukUlkara aBipArxya taLeda. 
\num{7} udedxVsha; Ashaya; eNike: \eng{will this meet your views?} idu nimamx udedxVshagaLige sarihoMdutatxdeye? 
\num{8} viVkaSxN; avaloVkana; pariVkaSxN; samIkaSxN; cAkuSxSa yA mAnasika samiVkeSx; kaNiNxniMda yA mAnasikavAgi pariVkiSxsuvudu, taniKe mADuvudu. 
\num{9} viVkaSxN; viVkaSxNAvakAsha: \eng{a view of the exhibition} parxdashaRnada viVkaSxNe, noVT.

\expl{}
\bmng

\banum

\alnum{b} (tiVmARnisuvAga, yAvudeV aMshavanunx) gamanadalilx, daqSiTxyalilx -- iTuTxkoMDiru. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{2} \eng{in view of} 
\banum
\alnum{a} daqSiTxpathadalilx yA pathakekx; kaNiNxge biVLuva sAthxnadalilx: \eng{we came in view of the church} A cacuR kaNiNxge biVLuva sAthxnakekx baMdevu. \eng{he stood in view of the audience} avanu perxVkaSxkara daqSiTxpathadalilx niMta. 
\alnum{b} daqSiTxyiMda; noVDidare; noVDidalilx; gamanisidare; parigaNisidare; kAraNdiMda: \eng{in view of the recent developments, we do not think this step advisable} ititxVcina GaTnegaLanunx noVDidare, parigaNisidare, I hejejx (kAyaRkarxma) vihitavAdadedxMdu namage toVruvudillx. 
\alnum{c} (\pArxparx) (muMde Aguvudanunx niriVkiSxsutAtx adakekx) pUvaRBAviyAgi. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} \eng{on view} noVDuvudakAkxgi, pariVkeSxgAgi, parishiVlnegAgi, avaloVkanakAkxgi -- parxdashiRsida. 
\num{4} \eng{private view} (citarx parxdashaRnada \vi) (senxVhitaru, vimashaRkaru, \mo) ApatxvagaRkekx mAtarx parxdashaRna; KAsagi parxdashaRna. 
\num{5} \eng{take a \hyperref{kandict_d.pdf}{D}{dim(1) nuga}{${}^1$dim} view of.}

\num{8} \eng{to the view} bahiraMgavAgi; parxtayxkaSxvAgi; parxkaTvAgi; ellxrigU kANuvaMte.

\expl{(\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{visited;} \vakaq\}
\eng{visiting}). \bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (senxVhadiMda, gwrava toVrisalu yA mayARdegAgi, kAyARthaRvAgi, yAvudeV udedxVshakAkxgi yA sAvxthaRkAkxgi) noVDalu, kANlu --baru yA hoVgu; BeVTi -- mADu, koDu. 
\num{2} (adhikArada vatiyiMda parishiVlnegAgi, meVlivxcAraNegAgi, samAloVcanegAgi yA parisithxtiyanunx saripaDisuvudakAkxgi) noVDalu baru yA hoVgu; BeVTi mADu, koDu. 
\num{3} (roVga, vipatutx, \mo vugaLa \vi) baDi; tagulu; eragu: \eng{the whole village was visited by (\engit{or} with) the plague} A iDiV haLiLxge pelxVgf baDiyitu, tagulitu. 
\numi{4} (\beY) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (vayxkitxyanunx, pApavanunx) daMDisu. 
\alnum{b} (pApakAkxgi vayxkitxge) shikeSxyanunx koDu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{5} (\pArxparx) (mukitx \mo vanunx niVDi) (vayxkitxyanunx) saMtayisu; samAdhAna mADu; anugarxhisu; kApADu. 
\num{6} (obabx vayxkitxya jote tAtAkxlikavAgi oMdu sathxLadalilx) iru; taMgu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
BeVTiyAgu; BeVTigAranAgu. 
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
 \eng{visit with} 
\banum

\alnum{b} (vayxkitxyoDane) mAtanADu; haraTe hoDe; saMBASisu. 
\eanum
\emng

\num{4} veYdayx, daMtaveYdayx, \mo varalilxge mADida BeVTi.

\hyperlink{viva voce(2)}{\textcolor{superscript}{$^2$}\eng{viva voce}}\quad\hyperlink{viva-voce(1)}{\textcolor{superscript}{$^4$}\eng{viva-voce}}\quad}\pron{veYvavoVsi(ci)} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
 (vishavxvidAyxnilya, kAleVju, \mo vugaLa) vAkapxriVkeSx; bAyimAtina, mwKika -- pariVkeSx. 
\emng

\bentry

\emng

\bentry 
\word{vivid} 
\pron{viviDf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (beLaku, baNNx -- ivugaLa \vi) ujajxvXlvAda; parxkAshamAnavAda; edudxkANuva; kaDu: \eng{a vivid flash of lightning} miMcina ujajxvXlvAda hoLapu. \eng{a vivid green} kaDuhasuru. 
\num{2} (vayxkitxya \vi) lvalvikeya; ulAlxsaBaritanAda; shakitxshAliyAda. 
\num{3} (manashashxkitx, manasisxna meVlAda pariNAma, vaNRne -- ivugaLa \vi) sapxSaTx(vAda); vishada; suPxT; suvayxkatx; kaNiNxge kaTuTxvaMtha: \eng{he has a vivid imagination} avanige vishadavAda kalpxne ide. \eng{a vivid description} sapxSaTx vaNRne. \eng{I have a vivid recollection of the scene} nanage A daqshayxda sapxSaTxvAda nenapide. 
\enum

\bentry 
\word{vocabulary} 
\pron{vakAYxbauyxlri} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{vocabularies}). }
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} shabadxkoVsha; padapaTiTx: 
\banum
\alnum{a} oMdu BASeya yA oMdu pusatxkadalilx yA oMdu vijAcnxna, kale, shAsatxrX, \mo vugaLalilx yA obabx garxMthakataRnu baLasiruva padagaLu: \eng{the ever-increasing scientific vocabulary} sadA hecucxtatxleV iruva vijAcnxna padakoVsha. 
\alnum{b} akArAdiyAgi joVDisi, athaRgaLanunx yA anuvAdagaLanunx niVDiruva A padagaLa paTiTx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} obabxna shabadx -- saMpatutx, BaMDAra; vayxkitxyobabxnige tiLidiruva padagaLa vAyxpitx: \eng{his vocabulary is limited} avana shabadxsaMpatutx parimitavAdadudx. \eng{a word not found in the Chaucerian vocabulary} cAsarf kaviya shabadxBaMDAradalilx kaMDubarada oMdu pada. 
\num{3} kalArUpagaLa, sheYlirUpagaLa yA taMtarxgaLa (\kanmu\ bAYxle \mo\ naqtayxgaLa nAyxsagaLa) taMDa. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\gl{\nA}

\num{2} deYvaperxVraNe; deVvAdiSaTxvAda vaqtitx; deYva saMkalipxta kAyaR yA sithxti; deYvaperxVritaveMdu BAvitavAda vaqtitx yA udoyxVga: \eng{he felt no vocation for the ministry} pAdirxvaqtitxge avanalilx deYvaperxVraNeyiralillx. 
\num{3} (aMtaH)perxVraNe; parxvaqtitx; olvu: \eng{he has no vocation to literature} avanige sAhitayxracaneyatatx olvillx, parxvaqtitxyillx. 
\num{4} (\kanmu\ sharxdedhx toVrabeVkeMdu parigaNitavAda) vayxkitxya -- vaqtitx, kasubau, udoyxVga. 
\num{5} yAvudeV udoyxVga, vaqtitx, kasubau.

\emng

\bentry 
\word[voice(1)]{voice} 
\pron{vAyfsx} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (dhavxninALadalilx huTiTx bAyalilx horaDuva, \kanmu\ manuSayxra) dhavxni; dani; shabadx; kaMTha; gaMTlu: \eng{I heard a voice} nanage oMdu dhavxni keVLisitu. \eng{he spoke in a low voice} avanu meludaniyalilx mAtanADida. \eng{I did not recognize her voice} nanage Akeya dhavxniya guruteV sigalillx. \eng{the voice of the cuckoo} koVkil dhavxni; koVkilkaMTha. \eng{he has such a loud voice} avanige aSoTxMdu gaTiTxyAda dhavxni ide. 
\numi{2} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (mAtina \vi) ucAcxraNe. 
\alnum{b} (hADina \vi) kaMTha; shAriVra. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} gaMTlu; kaMTha; dhavxni(shakitx); shAriVra(bal): \eng{has lost her voice} avaLa shAriVra kugigxhoVgide. 
\num{4} mAtu; dani; nAlige; vAkukx; vANi; \kanmu\ ADida yA bareda padagaLu: \eng{he gave voice to his indignation in a pamphlet} avanu oMdu kiruhotatxgeyalilx tananx nAyxyavAda koVpavanunx padagaLalilx horageDahida, koVpakekx nAlige koTTx. \eng{the dog gave voice to its joy} A nAyi tananx AnaMdavanunx kUginalilx sUcisitu. 
\numi{5} 
\banum
\alnum{a} mAtu; dhavxni; vayxkatxpaDisida aBipArxya. 
\alnum{b} aBipArxya koDuva hakukx: \eng{I have no voice in this matter} I viSayadalilx nanage aBipArxya koDuva hakikxllx. 
\alnum{c} vANi; aBipArxya vayxkatxpaDisalu baLasuva vayxkitx yA sAdhana. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} (\dhavxni) GoVSavaNR; dhavxnitaMtugaLa anuraNnadiMda yA kaMpanadiMda huTuTxva dhavxni. 
\num{7} (\vAyx) (kirxyApadada) kataRri, kamaRNi yA BAveV -- parxyoVga rUpa; kataRqvigU kirxyegU iruva saMbaMdhavanunx sUcisuva kirxyArUpagaLalilx oMdu. 
\numi{8} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\saM) saMgiVta kaqtiya hADuva yA gAyana BAga. 
\alnum{b} (\saM) PUZyxgf eMba saMgiVta kaqtiya gAyanAMsha. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{9} (\sA\ \bava dalilx) deYvavANi; ashariVra, agoVcara -- dhavxni; adaqshayx Atamxvu mAgaRdashaRna mADalu nuDidudeMdu naMbalAda mAtu, dhavxni, shabadx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{at the \hyperref{kandict_t.pdf}{T}{top(1)16}{${}^1$top} of one's voice.} 
\numi{2} \eng{in (good) voice} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (mAtanADuvudaralilx) oLeLxya ucAcxraN shakitxyuLaLx. 
\alnum{b} (hADuvudaralilx) (utatxma) kaMThavuLaLx, shAriVravuLaLx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} \eng{the voice of God} deYvavANi; deYva -- saMkalpx; korxVdha, shApa, \mo vugaLa aBivayxkitx. 
\num{4} \eng{with one voice} EkakaMThadiMda; EkABipArxyadiMda; okokxraliniMda; omamxtadiMda.

\bentry 
\word[voluntary(1)]{voluntary} 
\pron{vAlMTri} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} savx, savxyaM -- perxVrita; savxMta iSaTxdiMda, icePxyiMda -mADida yA mADuva yA mADaballx; nibaRMdhitavAgi yA kaDADxyavAgi irada; savxsaMtoVSadiMda yA savxtaH mADida: \eng{voluntary contribution} savxsaMtoVSada kANike. 
\num{2} udedxVshapUvaRkavAda; icAPxpUvaRkavAda: \eng{voluntary waste} (hiDuvaLidAra yA bADigedAra mADida) udedxVshapUvaRkavAda nAsha, halAku. 
\num{3} veVtanarahita; saMbaLa illxda yA tegedukoLaLxda : \eng{voluntary work} veVtanarahita kelsa, udoyxVga. 
\num{4} (saMsethxya \vi) savxyaMperxVrita dAna, vaMtige, caMdA yA deVNigegaLiMda naDeyuva yA naDesuva. 
\num{5} (\birx) (shAleya \vi) savxyaMseVvA saMGavoMdu kaTiTxda Adare sathxLiVya shikaSxN pArxdhikAravoMdu naDesuva, nivaRhisuva. 
\num{6} savxyaMseVveya; savxyaMperxVritavAgi mADida, utApxdisida, \mo. 
\num{7} (calne, mAMsaKMDa yA aMgada \vi) saMkalpxpUvaRkavAda; icAPxniyaMtirxtavAda. 
\num{8} (aparAdhiya tapopxpipxgeya \vi) (bedarike, parxloVBana, \mo vugaLiMda Agirade) savxperxVraNeyiMdAda; KududxrAjiyiMda mADida: \eng{voluntary confession} savxyaMperxVrita tapopxpipxge. (\nAyxshA) (Asitx vagARvaNe yA iSaTxpatarxda parxkAra koDuvudara \vi) muPatAtxda; parxtiPalvAgi haN yA beVrAvudeV parihAra bayasade koTTx. 
\num{10} sahaj parxvaqtitxya; aperxVritavAda. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry

\bentry

\pron{voVTf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} voVTu; (aBi)mata; aBayxthiRyanunx Ayekx mADuvudu, kAnUnanunx maMjUru mADuvudu, TharAvanunx opu pxvudu, \mo\ saMdaBaRgaLalilx matadAna patarxda meVle gurutisuvudu, keYetutxvudu, kUguvudu yA beVrAvudeV riVtiyalilx niVDuva aBipArxya: \eng{I shall give my vote to (\engit{or} for) the Labour candidate} nAnu kAmiRka pakaSxda aBayxthiRge yA aBayxthiRya paravAgi nananx mata niVDutetxVne. \eng{the resolution was put to the vote and passed without a dissent vote} A TharAvanunx voVTige hAkalAgi Binanxmatavillxde opapxlAyitu. 
\numi{2} (\birx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (sakARravu koVrida haNda \vi) (pAliRmeMTina) bahumatada anumoVdane. 
\alnum{b} bahumatABipArxya; bahumatadiMda vayxkatxvAda aBipArxya.

\numie
\num{3} voVTugaLa, matagaLa -- motatx; (oMdu pakaSx \mo vu yA oMdu pakaSx \mo vakekx koTTx yA koDabahudAda oTuTx voVTugaLu): \eng{he will lose the Labour vote} avanu kAmiRka pakaSxda matagaLanunx kaLedukoLuLxvanu. 
\num{4} (\kanmu\ rAjyxda cunAvaNeyalilx) matAdhikAra; matadAnada, voVTu mADuva -- hakukx: \eng{Swiss women now have the vote} sivxTZsxlRMDina heMgusarige Iga voVTina, voVTumADuva hakikxde. 
\num{5} voVTu ciVTi; voVTnunx gurutisalu baLasuva kAgada \mo vu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{put to a (\engit{or} the) vote} matakekx hAki niNRyisu, niNRyakekx oDuDx yA opipxsu. 
\num{2} \eng{take a vote on} (yAvudeV viSayada bagegx) mata tegeduko; (yAvudanenxV) matadAnada mUlka niNRyisu. 
\num{3} \eng{vote of censure} = \hyperlink{vote1 pagu5}{\pagu \eng{(5)}.} 
\num{4} \eng{vote of confidence} vishAvxsa mata; ADaLita pakaSxvanunx adhikasaMKAyxtaru beMbalisuvareMdu toVrisuva bahumata. 
\hypertarget{vote1 pagu5}{} 
\num{5} \eng{vote of no confidence} avishAvxsa mata; ADaLita pakaSxvanunx adhika saMKAyxtaru beMbalisuvudilalxveMdu sUcisuva bahumata.

\emng

\bentry
\word[vote(2)]{vote} 
\pron{voVTf} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} voVTumADu; matahAku; bahumatadiMda 
\banum
\alnum{a} kAnUnu mADu. 
\alnum{b} TharAvanunx anumoVdisu. 
\alnum{c} haN maMjUru mADu. 
\alnum{d} vayxkitxyanunx samiti \mo vugaLa sadasayxnanAnxgi cunAyisu yA samiti \mo vugaLa sadasayxtavxdiMda vajAmADu: \eng{was voted off (\engit{or} voted out of) the committee} bahumata hAki avananunx samitiyiMda vajA mADalAyitu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (\AmA) savaRsamamxtiyiMda, savARnumatadiMda -- sAru, GoVSisu; sAmAnAyxBipArxyavAgi heVLu: \eng{the scheme was voted a failure} A yoVjne viPalvAyiteMdu (savaRsamamxtiyiMda) sAralAyitu.

\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}

\gl{\pagu}

\numi{3} \eng{vote out} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (vayxkitxyanunx samiti \mo vugaLa) sadasayxtavxdiMda vajAmADu, horadUDu. 
\alnum{b} = \hyperlink{vote2 pagu1}{\pagu \eng{(1)}.}

\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
 valkxniVkarisu; gaMdhaka saMsAkxra koDu; rababxrf yA rababxrfnaMtha sAmagirxya sithxtisAthxpakatavxvanUnx balvanUnx hecicxsalu \kanmu\ hecicxna tApadalilx, gaMdhaka \mo vugaLiMda adanunx saMsakxrisu. 
\emng
\eentry

\emng

\bentry
\word{vulgar} 
\pron{valgxrf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} pAmara jnateya; jnasAmAnayxra. 
\num{2} nayanAjUkillxda; oraToraTAda; asaMsakxqqta; gArxmayx; asaBayx; kiVLuriVtiya; pArxkaqta: \eng{vulgar expressions} gArxmayx padagaLu. \eng{vulgar mind} asaMsakxqqta manasusx. \eng{vulgar tastes} kiVLu, halAkx -- aBirucigaLu. \eng{vulgar finery} oraToraTAda alMkAra. 
\num{3} sAmAnayx; baLakeya; rUDhiya; cAlitxyalilxruva; parxcalitavAda: \eng{vulgar errors} sAmAnayx doVSagaLu; rUDhiya tapu pxgaLu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
 \eng{the vulgar tongue} (hiMde baLakeyalilxdadx paMDitaBASeyAda lAYxTinfge BinanxvAgi) deVsi; deVshiVya BASe; jnapadara, jnasAmAnayxra BASe. 
\emng
\eentry
